\subsection{Function Documentation}
\hypertarget{a00116_a6fb2873d35a8a8089842d81a70a54167}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!add\+Graph@{add\+Graph}}
\index{add\+Graph@{add\+Graph}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{add\+Graph}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf Q\+C\+P\+Graph} $\ast$ Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::add\+Graph (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Q\+C\+P\+Axis} $\ast$}]{key\+Axis = {\ttfamily 0}, }
\item[{{\bf Q\+C\+P\+Axis} $\ast$}]{value\+Axis = {\ttfamily 0}}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_a6fb2873d35a8a8089842d81a70a54167}


Creates a new graph inside the plot. 

If {\itshape key\+Axis} and {\itshape value\+Axis} are left unspecified (0), the bottom (x\+Axis) is used as key and the left (y\+Axis) is used as value. If specified, {\itshape key\+Axis} and {\itshape value\+Axis} must reside in this \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot}.

{\itshape key\+Axis} will be used as key axis (typically \char`\"{}x\char`\"{}) and {\itshape value\+Axis} as value axis (typically \char`\"{}y\char`\"{}) for the graph.

Returns a pointer to the newly created graph.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_ab2463cfbef0d48d1829418647431bf35}{graph}, \hyperlink{a00116_a7d9b4d19114b2fde60f0233eeb0aa682}{graph\+Count}, \hyperlink{a00116_a9554b3d2d5b10c0f884bd4010b6c192c}{remove\+Graph}, \hyperlink{a00116_ab0f3abff2d2f7df3668b5836f39207fa}{clear\+Graphs} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Definition at line \hyperlink{a00115_source_l06688}{6688} of file \hyperlink{a00115_source}{qcustomplot.\+cpp}.

\index{add\+Plottable@{add\+Plottable}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{add\+Plottable}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::add\+Plottable (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable} $\ast$}]{plottable}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_ab7ad9174f701f9c6f64e378df77927a6}


Adds the specified plottable to the plot and, if \hyperlink{a00116_ad8858410c2db47b7104040a3aa61c3fc}{set\+Auto\+Add\+Plottable\+To\+Legend} is enabled, to the legend. 

\hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} takes ownership of the plottable.

Returns true on success, i.\+e. when {\itshape plottable} wasn't already added to the plot and the parent plot of {\itshape plottable} is this \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} (the latter is controlled by what axes the plottable was passed in the constructor).

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

       (via QCPLayerable constructor)}

\hypertarget{a00116_a6f4fa624af060bc5919c5f266cf426a0}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!after\+Replot@{after\+Replot}}
\index{after\+Replot@{after\+Replot}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{after\+Replot}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::after\+Replot (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{a00116_a6f4fa624af060bc5919c5f266cf426a0}


This signal is emitted immediately after a replot has taken place (caused by a call to the slot \hyperlink{a00116_a563540b54b2a09c8ef092d42e9621f42}{replot}). 

It is safe to mutually connect the replot slot with this signal on two Q\+Custom\+Plots to make them replot synchronously (i.\+e. it won't cause an infinite recursion).

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_a563540b54b2a09c8ef092d42e9621f42}{replot}, \hyperlink{a00116_a0cd30e29b73efd6afe096e44bc5956f5}{before\+Replot} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\item[{Q\+Mouse\+Event $\ast$}]{event}

This signal is emitted when an axis is clicked. 

{\itshape event} is the mouse event that caused the click, {\itshape axis} is the axis that received the click and {\itshape part} indicates the part of the axis that was clicked.

\hypertarget{a00116_a0cd30e29b73efd6afe096e44bc5956f5}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!before\+Replot@{before\+Replot}}
\index{before\+Replot@{before\+Replot}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{before\+Replot}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::before\+Replot (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{a00116_a0cd30e29b73efd6afe096e44bc5956f5}


This signal is emitted immediately before a replot takes place (caused by a call to the slot \hyperlink{a00116_a563540b54b2a09c8ef092d42e9621f42}{replot}). 

It is safe to mutually connect the replot slot with this signal on two Q\+Custom\+Plots to make them replot synchronously (i.\+e. it won't cause an infinite recursion).

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_a563540b54b2a09c8ef092d42e9621f42}{replot}, \hyperlink{a00116_a6f4fa624af060bc5919c5f266cf426a0}{after\+Replot}

\hypertarget{a00116_a9d4808ab925b003054085246c92a257c}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!deselect\+All@{deselect\+All}}
\index{deselect\+All@{deselect\+All}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{deselect\+All}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::deselect\+All (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{a00116_a9d4808ab925b003054085246c92a257c}


Deselects everything in the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} (plottables, items, axes, legend and title). 

Since calling this function is not a user interaction, this does not emit the \hyperlink{a00116_a500c64a109bc773c973ad274f2fa4190}{selection\+Changed\+By\+User} signal. The individual selection\+Changed signals are emitted though, if the objects were previously selected.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_add9cc886ff5257f64fb4117cf6c135fe}{set\+Interactions}, \hyperlink{a00116_a6721b8c689bb7f2f400987e580508fe8}{selected\+Plottables}, \hyperlink{a00116_a3714adb0a26b8cf1bd70740a7ea464c4}{selected\+Items}, \hyperlink{a00116_aa6baf867e8beb96ed5bd471f83ece903}{selected\+Axes}, \hyperlink{a00116_a1ea6297300c3e2770e65f95836411755}{selected\+Legends} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Definition at line \hyperlink{a00115_source_l07189}{7189} of file \hyperlink{a00115_source}{qcustomplot.\+cpp}.

\hypertarget{a00116_a2ddc6669cdcd1224803f78e579858b16}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!draw\+Axis\+Background@{draw\+Axis\+Background}}
\index{draw\+Axis\+Background@{draw\+Axis\+Background}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{draw\+Axis\+Background}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::draw\+Axis\+Background (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Q\+C\+P\+Painter} $\ast$}]{painter}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}}\label{a00116_a2ddc6669cdcd1224803f78e579858b16}
If an axis background is provided via \hyperlink{a00116_a010330bf3686716b9f7d643b3f5205db}{set\+Axis\+Background}, this function first buffers the scaled version depending on \hyperlink{a00116_a55ad8c13d7db8b5c2f15d694773a43a3}{set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled} and \hyperlink{a00116_a82920d0db6cc36214dc4a9dfe386d1a1}{set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode} and then draws it inside the current axis\+Rect with the provided {\itshape painter}. The scaled version is buffered in m\+Scaled\+Axis\+Background to prevent the need for rescaling at every redraw. It is only updated, when the axis\+Rect has changed in a way that requires a rescale of the background pixmap (this is dependant on the \hyperlink{a00116_a82920d0db6cc36214dc4a9dfe386d1a1}{set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode}), or when a differend axis backgroud was set.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_a2e9b3d14dffa43c79835869d488936c9}{draw}, \hyperlink{a00116_a010330bf3686716b9f7d643b3f5205db}{set\+Axis\+Background}, \hyperlink{a00116_a55ad8c13d7db8b5c2f15d694773a43a3}{set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled}, \hyperlink{a00116_a82920d0db6cc36214dc4a9dfe386d1a1}{set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Definition at line \hyperlink{a00115_source_l08090}{8090} of file \hyperlink{a00115_source}{qcustomplot.\+cpp}.

\hypertarget{a00116_aa1ad9839539b4cdf9f7da768336650f2}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!handle\+Item\+Selection@{handle\+Item\+Selection}}
\index{handle\+Item\+Selection@{handle\+Item\+Selection}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{handle\+Item\+Selection}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::handle\+Item\+Selection (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Q\+Mouse\+Event $\ast$}]{event, }
\item[{bool}]{additive\+Selection, }
\item[{bool \&}]{modified}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}}\label{a00116_aa1ad9839539b4cdf9f7da768336650f2}
Handles a mouse {\itshape event} for the item selection interaction. Returns true, when a selectable item was hit by the mouse event. The output variable {\itshape modified} is set to true when the selection state of an item has changed.

When {\itshape additive\+Selecton} is true, any new selections become selected in addition to the recent selections. The recent selections are not cleared. Further, clicking on one object multiple times in additive selection mode, toggles the selection of that object on and off.

To indicate that all items that are selectable shall be deselected, pass 0 as {\itshape event}.

Unlike for axis and legend selection, this function can't be exported to the respective class itself (i.\+e. \hyperlink{a00022}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Item}). The function needs to know the distance of the mouse event to all items in the plot, in order to choose the item with the smallest distance. This wouldn't work if it were local to a single item. 

Definition at line \hyperlink{a00115_source_l07917}{7917} of file \hyperlink{a00115_source}{qcustomplot.\+cpp}.



References \hyperlink{a00115_source_l06924}{item\+At()}, \hyperlink{a00116_source_l02117}{m\+Items}, \hyperlink{a00116_source_l00854}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Item\+::selected()}, and \hyperlink{a00115_source_l11112}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Item\+::set\+Selected()}.



Referenced by \hyperlink{a00115_source_l07691}{mouse\+Release\+Event()}.

07867       selectionFound = \textcolor{keyword}{true};

07872       \}
07873     \}

07883         \}
07884       \}
07885     \}
07886   \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{comment}{// event == 0, so deselect selectable plottables}
07887   \{
07888     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i=0; i<\hyperlink{a00116_a57ed6eb2e0a767a8344de45110a3e81d}{mPlottables}.size(); ++i)

07893         modified = \textcolor{keyword}{true};
07894       \}
07895     \}
07896   \}
07897   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} selectionFound;

\hypertarget{a00116_ae688ab743e775cd0c69941a082dd32e3}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!handle\+Title\+Selection@{handle\+Title\+Selection}}
\index{handle\+Title\+Selection@{handle\+Title\+Selection}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{handle\+Title\+Selection}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::handle\+Title\+Selection (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Q\+Mouse\+Event $\ast$}]{event, }
\item[{bool}]{additive\+Selection, }
\item[{bool \&}]{modified}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}}\label{a00116_ae688ab743e775cd0c69941a082dd32e3}
Handles a mouse {\itshape event} for the title selection interaction. Returns true, when the title was hit by the mouse event. The output variable {\itshape modified} is set to true when the selection state of the title has changed.

When {\itshape additive\+Selecton} is true, any new selections become selected in addition to the recent selections. The recent selections are not cleared. Further, clicking on one object multiple times in additive selection mode, toggles the selection of that object on and off.

To indicate that the title shall be deselected, pass 0 as {\itshape event}.

\hypertarget{a00116_a793e4b04e0ede11a733021907368fa83}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!item\+At@{item\+At}}
\index{item\+At@{item\+At}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{item\+At}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Item} $\ast$ Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::item\+At (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Q\+Point\+F \&}]{pos, }
\item[{bool}]{only\+Selectable = {\ttfamily false}}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_a793e4b04e0ede11a733021907368fa83}


Returns the item at the pixel position {\itshape pos}. 

Items that only consist of single lines (e.\+g. \hyperlink{a00036}{Q\+C\+P\+Item\+Line} or \hyperlink{a00034}{Q\+C\+P\+Item\+Curve}) have a tolerance band around them, see \hyperlink{a00116_a4dc31241d7b09680950e19e5f971ed93}{set\+Selection\+Tolerance}. If multiple items come into consideration, the one closest to {\itshape pos} is returned.

If {\itshape only\+Selectable} is true, only items that are selectable (\hyperlink{a00022_a8a8e32a55bc478b849756a78c2d87fd2}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Item\+::set\+Selectable}) are considered.

If there is no item at {\itshape pos}, the return value is 0.

\hypertarget{a00116_a79cff0baafbca10a3aaf694d2d3b9ab3}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!legend\+Click@{legend\+Click}}
\index{legend\+Click@{legend\+Click}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{legend\+Click}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::legend\+Click (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Q\+C\+P\+Legend} $\ast$}]{legend, }
\item[{{\bf Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Legend\+Item} $\ast$}]{item, }
\item[{Q\+Mouse\+Event $\ast$}]{event}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{a00116_a79cff0baafbca10a3aaf694d2d3b9ab3}


This signal is emitted when a legend (item) is clicked. 

{\itshape event} is the mouse event that caused the click, {\itshape legend} is the legend that received the click and {\itshape item} is the legend item that received the click. If only the legend and no item is clicked, {\itshape item} is 0 (e.\+g. a click inside the legend padding, which is not part of any item).

\hypertarget{a00116_a0250f835c044521df1619b132288bca7}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!legend\+Double\+Click@{legend\+Double\+Click}}
\index{legend\+Double\+Click@{legend\+Double\+Click}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{legend\+Double\+Click}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::legend\+Double\+Click (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Q\+C\+P\+Legend} $\ast$}]{legend, }
\item[{{\bf Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Legend\+Item} $\ast$}]{item, }
\item[{Q\+Mouse\+Event $\ast$}]{event}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{a00116_a0250f835c044521df1619b132288bca7}


This signal is emitted when a legend (item) is double clicked. 

{\itshape event} is the mouse event that caused the click, {\itshape legend} is the legend that received the click and {\itshape item} is the legend item that received the click. If only the legend and no item is clicked, {\itshape item} is 0 (e.\+g. a click inside the legend padding, which is not part of any item).

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_a79cff0baafbca10a3aaf694d2d3b9ab3}{legend\+Click} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\hypertarget{a00116_a4904f06d831afae29cd5d10e889388c3}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!minimum\+Size\+Hint@{minimum\+Size\+Hint}}
\index{minimum\+Size\+Hint@{minimum\+Size\+Hint}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{minimum\+Size\+Hint}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}Q\+Size Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::minimum\+Size\+Hint (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}}\label{a00116_a4904f06d831afae29cd5d10e889388c3}
Returns a minimum size hint of Q\+Size(50, 50). This prevents \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} from being collapsed to size/width zero when placed in a layout where other components try to take in as much space as possible (e.\+g. Q\+Mdi\+Area).

(To overwrite this minimum size hint of \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot}, simply call Q\+Widget\+::set\+Minimum\+Size in the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget.)

\hypertarget{a00116_a467e30feeea8ec0dd35f19ca32a55ba7}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event@{mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event}}

\subsubsection[{mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}virtual void mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Q\+Mouse\+Event $\ast$}]{event}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}}\label{a00116_a467e30feeea8ec0dd35f19ca32a55ba7}
\hypertarget{a00116_a742ca4f94688bed2a685fd8a56ce5704}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!mouse\+Move@{mouse\+Move}}
\index{mouse\+Move@{mouse\+Move}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{mouse\+Move}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::mouse\+Move (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Q\+Mouse\+Event $\ast$}]{event}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{a00116_a742ca4f94688bed2a685fd8a56ce5704}


This signal is emitted when the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} receives a mouse move event. 

It is emitted before the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} handles its range dragging mechanism, so a slot connected to this signal can still influence the behaviour e.\+g. with \hyperlink{a00116_aa0e1c44295da2706d0f12ad48f64b806}{set\+Range\+Drag}.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
It is discouraged to change the drag-\/axes with \hyperlink{a00116_a9fa10e826a174884391c1c839d52c0a3}{set\+Range\+Drag\+Axes} here, because the dragging starting point was saved the moment the mouse was pressed. Thus it only has a sensible meaning for the range drag axes that were set at that moment. If you want to change the drag axes, consider doing this in the \hyperlink{a00116_aca75bf9afb5dd19349c375de2a87a051}{mouse\+Press} signal instead. 
\end{DoxyWarning}


Definition at line \hyperlink{a00067_source_l02478}{2478} of file \hyperlink{a00067_source}{moc\+\_\+qcustomplot.\+cpp}.

This signal is emitted when the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} receives a mouse press event. 

It is emitted before the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} handles its range dragging mechanism, so a slot connected to this signal can still influence the behaviour e.\+g. with \hyperlink{a00116_aa0e1c44295da2706d0f12ad48f64b806}{set\+Range\+Drag} or \hyperlink{a00116_a9fa10e826a174884391c1c839d52c0a3}{set\+Range\+Drag\+Axes}. 

Definition at line \hyperlink{a00067_source_l02471}{2471} of file \hyperlink{a00067_source}{moc\+\_\+qcustomplot.\+cpp}.

This signal is emitted when the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} receives a mouse release event. 

It is emitted before the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} handles its selection mechanism, so a slot connected to this signal can still influence the behaviour e.\+g. with \hyperlink{a00116_add9cc886ff5257f64fb4117cf6c135fe}{set\+Interactions} or \hyperlink{a00024_a22c69299eb5569e0f6bf084877a37dc4}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable\+::set\+Selectable}.

\hypertarget{a00116_ac1d1bc6ae4e13616fb02cef6d9e2188e}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!plottable\+At@{plottable\+At}}
\index{plottable\+At@{plottable\+At}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{plottable\+At}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable} $\ast$ Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::plottable\+At (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Q\+Point\+F \&}]{pos, }
\item[{bool}]{only\+Selectable = {\ttfamily false}}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_ac1d1bc6ae4e13616fb02cef6d9e2188e}


Returns the plottable at the pixel position {\itshape pos}. 

Plottables that only consist of single lines (e.\+g. graphs) have a tolerance band around them, see \hyperlink{a00116_a4dc31241d7b09680950e19e5f971ed93}{set\+Selection\+Tolerance}. If multiple plottables come into consideration, the one closest to {\itshape pos} is returned.

If {\itshape only\+Selectable} is true, only plottables that are selectable (\hyperlink{a00024_a22c69299eb5569e0f6bf084877a37dc4}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable\+::set\+Selectable}) are considered.

If there is no plottable at {\itshape pos}, the return value is 0. 

Definition at line \hyperlink{a00115_source_l06606}{6606} of file \hyperlink{a00115_source}{qcustomplot.\+cpp}.



References \hyperlink{a00116_source_l01702}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis\+::axis\+Rect()}, \hyperlink{a00116_source_l00375}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable\+::key\+Axis()}, \hyperlink{a00116_source_l02115}{m\+Plottables}, \hyperlink{a00116_source_l02128}{m\+Selection\+Tolerance}, \hyperlink{a00116_source_l00377}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable\+::selectable()}, \hyperlink{a00024_a0fd218d6c4974b6ab05bd2f688818556}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable\+::select\+Test()}, and \hyperlink{a00116_source_l00376}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable\+::value\+Axis()}.

\hypertarget{a00116_a903561be895fb6528a770d66ac5e6713}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!remove\+Graph@{remove\+Graph}}
\index{remove\+Graph@{remove\+Graph}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{remove\+Graph}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::remove\+Graph (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Q\+C\+P\+Graph} $\ast$}]{graph}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_a903561be895fb6528a770d66ac5e6713}


Removes the specified {\itshape graph} from the plot and, if necessary, from the legend. 

If any other graphs in the plot have a channel fill set towards the removed graph, the channel fill property of those graphs is reset to zero (no channel fill).

Returns true on success.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_ab0f3abff2d2f7df3668b5836f39207fa}{clear\+Graphs} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}

\hypertarget{a00116_a40f75e342c5eaab6a86066a42a0e2a94}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!remove\+Layer@{remove\+Layer}}
\index{remove\+Layer@{remove\+Layer}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{remove\+Layer}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::remove\+Layer (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Q\+C\+P\+Layer} $\ast$}]{layer}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_a40f75e342c5eaab6a86066a42a0e2a94}


Removes the specified {\itshape layer} and returns true on success. 

All layerables (e.\+g. plottables and items) on the removed layer will be moved to the layer below {\itshape layer}. If {\itshape layer} is the bottom layer, the layerables are moved to the layer above. In both cases, the total rendering order of all layerables in the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} is preserved.

If {\itshape layer} is the current layer (\hyperlink{a00116_a23a4d3cadad1a0063c5fe19aac5659e6}{set\+Current\+Layer}), the layer below (or above, if bottom layer) becomes the new current layer.

Note that it is not possible to remove the last layer.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_a1b7efcbaf6ed6181f1a28f3d486f8837}{layer}, \hyperlink{a00116_acfae623ec58e4f9e35014062580e4720}{add\+Layer}, \hyperlink{a00116_ad18d1ff9086f2e658b81d67d3c84a0c3}{move\+Layer} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\hypertarget{a00116_a563540b54b2a09c8ef092d42e9621f42}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!replot@{replot}}
\index{replot@{replot}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{replot}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::replot (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{a00116_a563540b54b2a09c8ef092d42e9621f42}


Causes a complete replot (axes, labels, graphs, etc.) into the internal buffer. 

Finally, update() is called, to redraw the buffer on the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget surface.

Before the replot happens, the signal \hyperlink{a00116_a0cd30e29b73efd6afe096e44bc5956f5}{before\+Replot} is emitted. After the replot, \hyperlink{a00116_a6f4fa624af060bc5919c5f266cf426a0}{after\+Replot} is emitted. It is safe to mutually connect the replot slot with any of those two signals on two Q\+Custom\+Plots to make them replot synchronously (i.\+e. it won't cause an infinite recursion). 

Definition at line \hyperlink{a00115_source_l07221}{7221} of file \hyperlink{a00115_source}{qcustomplot.\+cpp}.



References \hyperlink{a00067_source_l02581}{after\+Replot()}, \hyperlink{a00067_source_l02575}{before\+Replot()}, \hyperlink{a00116_a2e9b3d14dffa43c79835869d488936c9}{draw()}, \hyperlink{a00116_source_l02114}{m\+Color}, \hyperlink{a00116_source_l02133}{m\+Paint\+Buffer}, \hyperlink{a00116_source_l02140}{m\+Plotting\+Hints}, and \hyperlink{a00116_source_l02137}{m\+Replotting}.

\subsubsection[{resize\+Event}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::resize\+Event (

\end{DoxyParamCaption}

Event handler for a resize of the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget. Causes the internal buffer to be resized to the new size. The viewport and the axis rect are resized appropriately. Finally a replot is performed.

\hypertarget{a00116_a6629d9e8e6da4bf18055ee0257fdce9a}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!save\+Bmp@{save\+Bmp}}
\index{save\+Bmp@{save\+Bmp}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{save\+Bmp}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::save\+Bmp (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Q\+String \&}]{file\+Name, }
\item[{int}]{width = {\ttfamily 0}, }
\item[{int}]{height = {\ttfamily 0}, }
\item[{double}]{scale = {\ttfamily 1.0}}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_a6629d9e8e6da4bf18055ee0257fdce9a}


Saves a B\+M\+P image file to {\itshape file\+Name} on disc. 

The output plot will have the dimensions {\itshape width} and {\itshape height} in pixels. If either {\itshape width} or {\itshape height} is zero, the exported image will have the same dimensions as the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget currently has. Line widths and texts etc. are not scaled up when larger widths/heights are used. If you want that effect, use the {\itshape scale} parameter.

For example, if you set both {\itshape width} and {\itshape height} to 100 and {\itshape scale} to 2, you will end up with an image file of size 200$\ast$200 in which all graphical elements are scaled up by factor 2 (line widths, texts, etc.). This scaling is not done by stretching a 100$\ast$100 image, the result will have full 200$\ast$200 pixel resolution.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
If calling this function inside the constructor of the parent of the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget (i.\+e. the \hyperlink{a00017}{Main\+Window} constructor, if \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} is inside the \hyperlink{a00017}{Main\+Window}), always provide explicit non-\/zero widths and heights. If you leave {\itshape width} or {\itshape height} as 0 (default), this function uses the current width and height of the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget. However, in Qt, these aren't defined yet inside the constructor, so you would get an image that has strange widths/heights.
\end{DoxyWarning}
The objects of the plot will appear in the current selection state. If you don't want any selected objects to be painted in their selected look, deselect everything with \hyperlink{a00116_a9d4808ab925b003054085246c92a257c}{deselect\+All} before calling this function.

Returns true on success. If this function fails, most likely the B\+M\+P format isn't supported by the system, see Qt docs about Q\+Image\+Writer\+::supported\+Image\+Formats().

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_a84e33ad7492180f20ff520e557ed102d}{save\+Pdf}, \hyperlink{a00116_a7636261aff1f6d25c9da749ece3fc8b8}{save\+Png}, \hyperlink{a00116_a490c722092d1771e8ce4a7a73dfd84ab}{save\+Jpg}, \hyperlink{a00116_ab528b84cf92baabe29b1d0ef2f77c93e}{save\+Rastered} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Definition at line \hyperlink{a00115_source_l07488}{7488} of file \hyperlink{a00115_source}{qcustomplot.\+cpp}.

\hypertarget{a00116_a490c722092d1771e8ce4a7a73dfd84ab}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!save\+Jpg@{save\+Jpg}}
\index{save\+Jpg@{save\+Jpg}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{save\+Jpg}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::save\+Jpg (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Q\+String \&}]{file\+Name, }
\item[{int}]{width = {\ttfamily 0}, }
\item[{int}]{height = {\ttfamily 0}, }
\item[{double}]{scale = {\ttfamily 1.0}, }
\item[{int}]{quality = {\ttfamily -\/1}}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_a490c722092d1771e8ce4a7a73dfd84ab}


Saves a J\+P\+G image file to {\itshape file\+Name} on disc. 

The output plot will have the dimensions {\itshape width} and {\itshape height} in pixels. If either {\itshape width} or {\itshape height} is zero, the exported image will have the same dimensions as the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget currently has. Line widths and texts etc. are not scaled up when larger widths/heights are used. If you want that effect, use the {\itshape scale} parameter.

For example, if you set both {\itshape width} and {\itshape height} to 100 and {\itshape scale} to 2, you will end up with an image file of size 200$\ast$200 in which all graphical elements are scaled up by factor 2 (line widths, texts, etc.). This scaling is not done by stretching a 100$\ast$100 image, the result will have full 200$\ast$200 pixel resolution.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
If calling this function inside the constructor of the parent of the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget (i.\+e. the \hyperlink{a00017}{Main\+Window} constructor, if \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} is inside the \hyperlink{a00017}{Main\+Window}), always provide explicit non-\/zero widths and heights. If you leave {\itshape width} or {\itshape height} as 0 (default), this function uses the current width and height of the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget. However, in Qt, these aren't defined yet inside the constructor, so you would get an image that has strange widths/heights.
\end{DoxyWarning}
The objects of the plot will appear in the current selection state. If you don't want any selected objects to be painted in their selected look, deselect everything with \hyperlink{a00116_a9d4808ab925b003054085246c92a257c}{deselect\+All} before calling this function.

J\+P\+G compression can be controlled with the {\itshape quality} parameter which must be between 0 and 100 or -\/1 to use the default setting.

Returns true on success. If this function fails, most likely the J\+P\+G format isn't supported by the system, see Qt docs about Q\+Image\+Writer\+::supported\+Image\+Formats().

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\hypertarget{a00116_a84e33ad7492180f20ff520e557ed102d}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!save\+Pdf@{save\+Pdf}}
\index{save\+Pdf@{save\+Pdf}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{save\+Pdf}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::save\+Pdf (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Q\+String \&}]{file\+Name, }
\item[{bool}]{no\+Cosmetic\+Pen = {\ttfamily false}, }
\item[{int}]{width = {\ttfamily 0}, }
\item[{int}]{height = {\ttfamily 0}}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_a84e33ad7492180f20ff520e557ed102d}


Saves a P\+D\+F with the vectorized plot to the file {\itshape file\+Name}. 

The axis ratio as well as the scale of texts and lines will be derived from the specified {\itshape width} and {\itshape height}. This means, the output will look like the normal on-\/screen output of a \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget with the corresponding pixel width and height. If either {\itshape width} or {\itshape height} is zero, the exported image will have the same dimensions as the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget currently has.

{\itshape no\+Cosmetic\+Pen} disables the use of cosmetic pens when drawing to the P\+D\+F file. Cosmetic pens are pens with numerical width 0, which are always drawn as a one pixel wide line, no matter what zoom factor is set in the P\+D\+F-\/\+Viewer. For more information about cosmetic pens, see \hyperlink{a00060}{Q\+Painter} and Q\+Pen documentation.

The objects of the plot will appear in the current selection state. So when you don't want e.\+g. selected axes to be painted in their selected look, deselect everything with \hyperlink{a00116_a9d4808ab925b003054085246c92a257c}{deselect\+All} before calling this function.

Returns true on success.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If you plan on editing the exported P\+D\+F file with a vector graphics editor like Inkscape, it is advised to set {\itshape no\+Cosmetic\+Pen} to true to avoid losing those cosmetic lines (which might be quite many, because cosmetic pens are the default for e.\+g. axes and tick marks). \item If calling this function inside the constructor of the parent of the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget (i.\+e. the \hyperlink{a00017}{Main\+Window} constructor, if \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} is inside the \hyperlink{a00017}{Main\+Window}), always provide explicit non-\/zero widths and heights. If you leave {\itshape width} or {\itshape height} as 0 (default), this function uses the current width and height of the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget. However, in Qt, these aren't defined yet inside the constructor, so you would get an image that has strange widths/heights.\end{DoxyItemize}

\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_a7636261aff1f6d25c9da749ece3fc8b8}{save\+Png}, \hyperlink{a00116_a6629d9e8e6da4bf18055ee0257fdce9a}{save\+Bmp}, \hyperlink{a00116_a490c722092d1771e8ce4a7a73dfd84ab}{save\+Jpg}, \hyperlink{a00116_ab528b84cf92baabe29b1d0ef2f77c93e}{save\+Rastered} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Definition at line \hyperlink{a00115_source_l07350}{7350} of file \hyperlink{a00115_source}{qcustomplot.\+cpp}.

\hypertarget{a00116_a7636261aff1f6d25c9da749ece3fc8b8}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!save\+Png@{save\+Png}}
\index{save\+Png@{save\+Png}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{save\+Png}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::save\+Png (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Q\+String \&}]{file\+Name, }
\item[{int}]{width = {\ttfamily 0}, }
\item[{int}]{height = {\ttfamily 0}, }
\item[{double}]{scale = {\ttfamily 1.0}, }
\item[{int}]{quality = {\ttfamily -\/1}}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_a7636261aff1f6d25c9da749ece3fc8b8}


Saves a P\+N\+G image file to {\itshape file\+Name} on disc. 

The output plot will have the dimensions {\itshape width} and {\itshape height} in pixels. If either {\itshape width} or {\itshape height} is zero, the exported image will have the same dimensions as the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget currently has. Line widths and texts etc. are not scaled up when larger widths/heights are used. If you want that effect, use the {\itshape scale} parameter.

For example, if you set both {\itshape width} and {\itshape height} to 100 and {\itshape scale} to 2, you will end up with an image file of size 200$\ast$200 in which all graphical elements are scaled up by factor 2 (line widths, texts, etc.). This scaling is not done by stretching a 100$\ast$100 image, the result will have full 200$\ast$200 pixel resolution.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
If calling this function inside the constructor of the parent of the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget (i.\+e. the \hyperlink{a00017}{Main\+Window} constructor, if \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} is inside the \hyperlink{a00017}{Main\+Window}), always provide explicit non-\/zero widths and heights. If you leave {\itshape width} or {\itshape height} as 0 (default), this function uses the current width and height of the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget. However, in Qt, these aren't defined yet inside the constructor, so you would get an image that has strange widths/heights.
\end{DoxyWarning}
The objects of the plot will appear in the current selection state. If you don't want any selected objects to be painted in their selected look, deselect everything with \hyperlink{a00116_a9d4808ab925b003054085246c92a257c}{deselect\+All} before calling this function.

If you want the plot to be painted in a P\+N\+G with transparent background, call \hyperlink{a00116_a858bbcf98637471449e438304a00624b}{set\+Color} with a transparent color, e.\+g. Qt\+::transparent, before saving.

P\+N\+G compression can be controlled with the {\itshape quality} parameter which must be between 0 and 100 or -\/1 to use the default setting.

Returns true on success. If this function fails, most likely the P\+N\+G format isn't supported by the system, see Qt docs about Q\+Image\+Writer\+::supported\+Image\+Formats().

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_a84e33ad7492180f20ff520e557ed102d}{save\+Pdf}, \hyperlink{a00116_a6629d9e8e6da4bf18055ee0257fdce9a}{save\+Bmp}, \hyperlink{a00116_a490c722092d1771e8ce4a7a73dfd84ab}{save\+Jpg}, \hyperlink{a00116_ab528b84cf92baabe29b1d0ef2f77c93e}{save\+Rastered} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\hypertarget{a00116_ab528b84cf92baabe29b1d0ef2f77c93e}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!save\+Rastered@{save\+Rastered}}
\index{save\+Rastered@{save\+Rastered}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{save\+Rastered}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::save\+Rastered (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Q\+String \&}]{file\+Name, }
\item[{int}]{width, }
\item[{int}]{height, }
\item[{double}]{scale, }
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{format, }
\item[{int}]{quality = {\ttfamily -\/1}}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_ab528b84cf92baabe29b1d0ef2f77c93e}


Saves the plot to a rastered image file {\itshape file\+Name} in the image format {\itshape format}. 

The plot is sized to {\itshape width} and {\itshape height} in pixels and scaled with {\itshape scale}. (width 100 and scale 2.\+0 lead to a full resolution file with width 200) If the {\itshape format} supports compression, {\itshape quality} may be between 0 and 100 to control it.

Returns true on success. If this function fails, most likely the given {\itshape format} isn't supported by the system, see Qt docs about Q\+Image\+Writer\+::supported\+Image\+Formats().

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_a6629d9e8e6da4bf18055ee0257fdce9a}{save\+Bmp}, \hyperlink{a00116_a490c722092d1771e8ce4a7a73dfd84ab}{save\+Jpg}, \hyperlink{a00116_a7636261aff1f6d25c9da749ece3fc8b8}{save\+Png} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\hypertarget{a00116_ad2a0493bdd01e7aa99a4209ae3a5b67b}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!selected\+Graphs@{selected\+Graphs}}
\index{selected\+Graphs@{selected\+Graphs}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{selected\+Graphs}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}Q\+List$<$ {\bf Q\+C\+P\+Graph} $\ast$ $>$ Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::selected\+Graphs (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_ad2a0493bdd01e7aa99a4209ae3a5b67b}


Returns a list of the selected graphs. 

If no graphs are currently selected, the list is empty.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Even if the returned list is empty, it might still be, that there are selected plottables in the plot that are not of type \hyperlink{a00031}{Q\+C\+P\+Graph} (e.\+g. \hyperlink{a00028}{Q\+C\+P\+Curve}, \hyperlink{a00027}{Q\+C\+P\+Bars}, etc.), see \hyperlink{a00116_a6721b8c689bb7f2f400987e580508fe8}{selected\+Plottables}. Of course, this only applies, if you actually add non-\/\+Q\+C\+P\+Graph plottables.
\end{DoxyNote}

\hyperlink{a00116_add9cc886ff5257f64fb4117cf6c135fe}{set\+Interactions}, \hyperlink{a00116_a6721b8c689bb7f2f400987e580508fe8}{selected\+Plottables}, \hyperlink{a00024_a22c69299eb5569e0f6bf084877a37dc4}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable\+::set\+Selectable}, \hyperlink{a00024_afbd5428c2952f59d952e11ab5cd79176}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable\+::set\+Selected}

This signal is emitted after the user has changed the selection in the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot}, e.\+g. 

by clicking. It is not emitted, when the selection state of an object has changed programmatically, e.\+g. by a direct call to set\+Selected() on a plottable or by calling \hyperlink{a00116_a9d4808ab925b003054085246c92a257c}{deselect\+All}.

See the documentation of \hyperlink{a00116_add9cc886ff5257f64fb4117cf6c135fe}{set\+Interactions} for how to find out which objects are currently selected.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_add9cc886ff5257f64fb4117cf6c135fe}{set\+Interactions}, \hyperlink{a00024_a3af66432b1dca93b28e00e78a8c7c1d9}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable\+::selection\+Changed}, \hyperlink{a00025_aece2d803d07dba9dc2ea96fcad186e34}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis\+::selection\+Changed}

\hypertarget{a00116_aeef813bcf7efab8e765f9f87ec454691}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!set\+Antialiased\+Element@{set\+Antialiased\+Element}}
\index{set\+Antialiased\+Element@{set\+Antialiased\+Element}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{set\+Antialiased\+Element}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::set\+Antialiased\+Element (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Q\+C\+P\+::\+Antialiased\+Element}}]{antialiased\+Element, }
\item[{bool}]{enabled = {\ttfamily true}}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_aeef813bcf7efab8e765f9f87ec454691}


Sets whether the specified {\itshape antialiased\+Element} is forcibly drawn antialiased. 

This overrides the antialiasing settings for whole element groups, normally controlled with the {\itshape set\+Antialiasing} function on the individual elements. If an element is neither specified in \hyperlink{a00116_af6f91e5eab1be85f67c556e98c3745e8}{set\+Antialiased\+Elements} nor in \hyperlink{a00116_ae10d685b5eabea2999fb8775ca173c24}{set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Elements}, the antialiasing setting on each individual element instance is used.

For example, if {\itshape enabled} is true and {\itshape antialiased\+Element} is \hyperlink{a00143_ae55dbe315d41fe80f29ba88100843a0ca4145e4251b0cf2dbedabeea0a38f84f6}{Q\+C\+P\+::ae\+Plottables}, all plottables will be drawn antialiased, no matter what the specific \hyperlink{a00044_a4fd43e89be4a553ead41652565ff0581}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable\+::set\+Antialiased} value was set to.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_afc657938a707c890e449ae89203a076d}{set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Element} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Definition at line \hyperlink{a00115_source_l06135}{6135} of file \hyperlink{a00115_source}{qcustomplot.\+cpp}.

Sets which elements are forcibly drawn antialiased as an or combination of \hyperlink{a00143_ae55dbe315d41fe80f29ba88100843a0c}{Q\+C\+P\+::\+Antialiased\+Element}. 

This overrides the antialiasing settings for whole element groups, normally controlled with the {\itshape set\+Antialiasing} function on the individual elements. If an element is neither specified in \hyperlink{a00116_af6f91e5eab1be85f67c556e98c3745e8}{set\+Antialiased\+Elements} nor in \hyperlink{a00116_ae10d685b5eabea2999fb8775ca173c24}{set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Elements}, the antialiasing setting on each individual element instance is used.

For example, if {\itshape antialiased\+Elements} contains \hyperlink{a00143_ae55dbe315d41fe80f29ba88100843a0ca4145e4251b0cf2dbedabeea0a38f84f6}{Q\+C\+P\+::ae\+Plottables}, all plottables will be drawn antialiased, no matter what the specific \hyperlink{a00044_a4fd43e89be4a553ead41652565ff0581}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable\+::set\+Antialiased} value was set to.

\hypertarget{a00116_a6e61739de7485e99171c0fd5a57e27aa}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!set\+Axis\+Background@{set\+Axis\+Background}}
\index{set\+Axis\+Background@{set\+Axis\+Background}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{set\+Axis\+Background}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::set\+Axis\+Background (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Q\+Pixmap \&}]{pm}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_a6e61739de7485e99171c0fd5a57e27aa}


Sets {\itshape pm} as the axis background pixmap. 

The axis background pixmap will be drawn inside the current axis rect, before anything else (e.\+g. the axes themselves, grids, graphs, etc.) is drawn. If the provided pixmap doesn't have the same size as the axis rect, scaling can be enabled with \hyperlink{a00116_a55ad8c13d7db8b5c2f15d694773a43a3}{set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled} and the scaling mode (i.\+e. whether and how the aspect ratio is preserved) can be set with \hyperlink{a00116_a82920d0db6cc36214dc4a9dfe386d1a1}{set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode}. To set all these options in one call, consider using the overloaded version of this function. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_a55ad8c13d7db8b5c2f15d694773a43a3}{set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled}, \hyperlink{a00116_a82920d0db6cc36214dc4a9dfe386d1a1}{set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Definition at line \hyperlink{a00115_source_l06222}{6222} of file \hyperlink{a00115_source}{qcustomplot.\+cpp}.

\hypertarget{a00116_a55ad8c13d7db8b5c2f15d694773a43a3}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled@{set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled}}
\index{set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled@{set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{bool}]{scaled}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_a55ad8c13d7db8b5c2f15d694773a43a3}


Sets whether the axis background pixmap shall be scaled to fit the current axis rect or not. 

If {\itshape scaled} is set to true, you may control whether and how the aspect ratio of the original pixmap is preserved with \hyperlink{a00116_a82920d0db6cc36214dc4a9dfe386d1a1}{set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode}.

Note that the scaled version of the original pixmap is buffered, so there is no performance penalty on replots, when enabling the scaling. (Except of course, the axis rect is continuously changed, but that's not very likely.)

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_a010330bf3686716b9f7d643b3f5205db}{set\+Axis\+Background}, \hyperlink{a00116_a82920d0db6cc36214dc4a9dfe386d1a1}{set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

If scaling of the axis background pixmap is enabled (\hyperlink{a00116_a55ad8c13d7db8b5c2f15d694773a43a3}{set\+Axis\+Background\+Scaled}), use this function to define whether and how the aspect ratio of the original pixmap passed to \hyperlink{a00116_a010330bf3686716b9f7d643b3f5205db}{set\+Axis\+Background} is preserved.

\subsubsection[{set\+Current\+Layer}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}bool Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::set\+Current\+Layer (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Q\+String \&}]{name}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_a73a6dc47c653bb6f8f030abca5a11852}


Sets the layer with the specified {\itshape name} to be the current layer. 

All newly created/added layerables (\hyperlink{a00044}{Q\+C\+P\+Layerable}), e.\+g. plottables and items, are initially placed on the current layer.

Returns true on success, i.\+e. if there is a layer with the specified {\itshape name} in the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot}.

\hypertarget{a00116_af9af5370ddc6e57f3e15809c1576cc38}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!set\+Interaction@{set\+Interaction}}
\index{set\+Interaction@{set\+Interaction}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{set\+Interaction}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void set\+Interaction (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Interaction \&}]{interaction, }
\item[{bool}]{enabled = {\ttfamily true}}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_af9af5370ddc6e57f3e15809c1576cc38}
\hypertarget{a00116_add9cc886ff5257f64fb4117cf6c135fe}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!set\+Interactions@{set\+Interactions}}
\index{set\+Interactions@{set\+Interactions}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{set\+Interactions}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::set\+Interactions (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Interactions \&}]{interactions}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_add9cc886ff5257f64fb4117cf6c135fe}


Sets the possible interactions of this \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} as an or-\/combination of Interaction enums. 

There are the following types of interactions\+:

{\bfseries Axis range manipulation} is controlled via i\+Range\+Drag and i\+Range\+Zoom. When the respective interaction is enabled, the user may drag axes ranges and zoom with the mouse wheel. For details how to control which axes the user may drag/zoom and in what orientations, see \hyperlink{a00116_aa0e1c44295da2706d0f12ad48f64b806}{set\+Range\+Drag}, \hyperlink{a00116_ad4a0919e471549a2daea517ce6538ad8}{set\+Range\+Zoom}, \hyperlink{a00116_a9fa10e826a174884391c1c839d52c0a3}{set\+Range\+Drag\+Axes}, \hyperlink{a00116_a9808f1736b8116c116bcccb53cdb210a}{set\+Range\+Zoom\+Axes}.

{\bfseries Plottable selection} is controlled by i\+Select\+Plottables. If i\+Select\+Plottables is set, the user may select plottables (e.\+g. graphs, curves, bars,...) by clicking on them or in their vicinity, see \hyperlink{a00116_a4dc31241d7b09680950e19e5f971ed93}{set\+Selection\+Tolerance}. Whether the user can actually select a plottable can further be restricted with the \hyperlink{a00024_a22c69299eb5569e0f6bf084877a37dc4}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable\+::set\+Selectable} function on the specific plottable. To find out whether a specific plottable is selected, call \hyperlink{a00024_ab901903adcb0e29467d63de72340ab29}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable\+::selected()}. To retrieve a list of all currently selected plottables, call \hyperlink{a00116_a6721b8c689bb7f2f400987e580508fe8}{selected\+Plottables}. If you're only interested in Q\+C\+P\+Graphs, you may use the convenience function \hyperlink{a00116_ad2a0493bdd01e7aa99a4209ae3a5b67b}{selected\+Graphs}.

{\bfseries Item selection} is controlled by i\+Select\+Items. If i\+Select\+Items is set, the user may select items (e.\+g. \hyperlink{a00036}{Q\+C\+P\+Item\+Line}, \hyperlink{a00041}{Q\+C\+P\+Item\+Text},...) by clicking on them or in their vicinity. To find out whether a specific item is selected, call \hyperlink{a00022_a225865808640d8d9a7dd19f09a2e93f2}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Item\+::selected()}. To retrieve a list of all currently selected items, call \hyperlink{a00116_a3714adb0a26b8cf1bd70740a7ea464c4}{selected\+Items}.

{\bfseries Axis selection} is controlled with i\+Select\+Axes. If i\+Select\+Axes is set, the user may select parts of the axes by clicking on them. What parts exactly (e.\+g. Axis base line, tick labels, axis label) are selectable can be controlled via \hyperlink{a00025_afa988209bf6519f63d6ef2e615dbe1ea}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis\+::set\+Selectable} for each axis. To retrieve a list of all axes that currently contain selected parts, call \hyperlink{a00116_aa6baf867e8beb96ed5bd471f83ece903}{selected\+Axes}. Which parts of an axis are selected, can be retrieved with \hyperlink{a00025_a534509949b91a6aa08e38cca48b62c9e}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis\+::selected()}.

{\bfseries Legend selection} is controlled with i\+Select\+Legend. If this is set, the user may select the legend itself or individual items by clicking on them. What parts exactly are selectable can be controlled via \hyperlink{a00045_aae042f6211e39305d13f7b18c1c301d9}{Q\+C\+P\+Legend\+::set\+Selectable}. To find out whether the legend or any child items are selected, check the value of \hyperlink{a00045_a10948e896935ad14f374e6f712afaae9}{Q\+C\+P\+Legend\+::selected}. To find out which child items are selected, call \hyperlink{a00045_ac93eaf236e911d67aa8b88942ef45c5e}{Q\+C\+P\+Legend\+::selected\+Items}.

{\bfseries Plot title selection} is controlled with i\+Select\+Title. If set, the user may select the plot title by clicking on it. To find out whether the title is currently selected, call Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::title\+Selected().

If the selection state has changed by user interaction, the \hyperlink{a00116_a500c64a109bc773c973ad274f2fa4190}{selection\+Changed\+By\+User} signal is emitted. Each selectable object additionally emits an individual selection\+Changed signal whenever their selection state has changed, i.\+e. not only by user interaction.

To allow multiple objects to be selected by holding the modifier set with \hyperlink{a00116_a8fc96e3b5138a06759a2a90c166df516}{set\+Multi\+Select\+Modifier}, set the flag i\+Multi\+Select.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
In addition to the selection mechanism presented here, \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} always emits corresponding signals, when an object is clicked or double clicked. see \hyperlink{a00116_a57e5efa8a854620e9bf62d31fc139f53}{plottable\+Click} and \hyperlink{a00116_af2e6f1cea923dae437681d01ce7d0c31}{plottable\+Double\+Click} for example.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_af9af5370ddc6e57f3e15809c1576cc38}{set\+Interaction}, \hyperlink{a00116_a4dc31241d7b09680950e19e5f971ed93}{set\+Selection\+Tolerance} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\hypertarget{a00116_a8fc96e3b5138a06759a2a90c166df516}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!set\+Multi\+Select\+Modifier@{set\+Multi\+Select\+Modifier}}

\subsubsection[{set\+Multi\+Select\+Modifier}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::set\+Multi\+Select\+Modifier (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Qt\+::\+Keyboard\+Modifier}]{modifier}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_a8fc96e3b5138a06759a2a90c166df516}


Sets the keyboard modifier that will be recognized as multi-\/select-\/modifier. 

If i\+Multi\+Select is specified in \hyperlink{a00116_add9cc886ff5257f64fb4117cf6c135fe}{set\+Interactions}, the user may select multiple objects by clicking on them one after the other while holding down {\itshape modifier}.

By default the multi-\/select-\/modifier is set to Qt\+::\+Control\+Modifier.

\hypertarget{a00116_a775bdcb6329d44701aeaa6135b0e5265}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!set\+No\+Antialiasing\+On\+Drag@{set\+No\+Antialiasing\+On\+Drag}}
\index{set\+No\+Antialiasing\+On\+Drag@{set\+No\+Antialiasing\+On\+Drag}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{set\+No\+Antialiasing\+On\+Drag}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::set\+No\+Antialiasing\+On\+Drag (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{bool}]{enabled}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_a775bdcb6329d44701aeaa6135b0e5265}


Sets whether antialiasing is disabled for all elements while the user is dragging axes ranges. 

If many objects, especially plottables, are normally drawn antialiased, this greatly improves performance during dragging. Thus it creates a more responsive user experience. As soon as the user stops dragging, the last replot is done with normal antialiasing, to restore high image quality.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_af6f91e5eab1be85f67c556e98c3745e8}{set\+Antialiased\+Elements}, \hyperlink{a00116_ae10d685b5eabea2999fb8775ca173c24}{set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Elements} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Definition at line \hyperlink{a00115_source_l06396}{6396} of file \hyperlink{a00115_source}{qcustomplot.\+cpp}.



References \hyperlink{a00116_source_l02131}{m\+No\+Antialiasing\+On\+Drag}.


\begin{DoxyCode}

06399 \}
\end{DoxyCode}
\hypertarget{a00116_afc657938a707c890e449ae89203a076d}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Element@{set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Element}}
\index{set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Element@{set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Element}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Element}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Element (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Q\+C\+P\+::\+Antialiased\+Element}}]{not\+Antialiased\+Element, }
\item[{bool}]{enabled = {\ttfamily true}}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_afc657938a707c890e449ae89203a076d}


Sets whether the specified {\itshape not\+Antialiased\+Element} is forcibly drawn not antialiased. 

This overrides the antialiasing settings for whole element groups, normally controlled with the {\itshape set\+Antialiasing} function on the individual elements. If an element is neither specified in \hyperlink{a00116_af6f91e5eab1be85f67c556e98c3745e8}{set\+Antialiased\+Elements} nor in \hyperlink{a00116_ae10d685b5eabea2999fb8775ca173c24}{set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Elements}, the antialiasing setting on each individual element instance is used.

For example, if {\itshape enabled} is true and {\itshape not\+Antialiased\+Element} is \hyperlink{a00143_ae55dbe315d41fe80f29ba88100843a0ca4145e4251b0cf2dbedabeea0a38f84f6}{Q\+C\+P\+::ae\+Plottables}, no plottables will be drawn antialiased, no matter what the specific \hyperlink{a00044_a4fd43e89be4a553ead41652565ff0581}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable\+::set\+Antialiased} value was set to.

if {\itshape enabled} is true and {\itshape not\+Antialiased\+Element} is already set with \hyperlink{a00116_aeef813bcf7efab8e765f9f87ec454691}{set\+Antialiased\+Element}, it is removed from there.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_aeef813bcf7efab8e765f9f87ec454691}{set\+Antialiased\+Element} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Definition at line \hyperlink{a00115_source_l06191}{6191} of file \hyperlink{a00115_source}{qcustomplot.\+cpp}.

\end{DoxyCode}
\hypertarget{a00116_ae10d685b5eabea2999fb8775ca173c24}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Elements@{set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Elements}}
\index{set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Elements@{set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Elements}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Elements}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Elements (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Q\+C\+P\+::\+Antialiased\+Elements \&}]{not\+Antialiased\+Elements}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_ae10d685b5eabea2999fb8775ca173c24}


Sets which elements are forcibly drawn not antialiased as an or combination of \hyperlink{a00143_ae55dbe315d41fe80f29ba88100843a0c}{Q\+C\+P\+::\+Antialiased\+Element}. 

This overrides the antialiasing settings for whole element groups, normally controlled with the {\itshape set\+Antialiasing} function on the individual elements. If an element is neither specified in \hyperlink{a00116_af6f91e5eab1be85f67c556e98c3745e8}{set\+Antialiased\+Elements} nor in \hyperlink{a00116_ae10d685b5eabea2999fb8775ca173c24}{set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Elements}, the antialiasing setting on each individual element instance is used.

For example, if {\itshape not\+Antialiased\+Elements} contains \hyperlink{a00143_ae55dbe315d41fe80f29ba88100843a0ca4145e4251b0cf2dbedabeea0a38f84f6}{Q\+C\+P\+::ae\+Plottables}, no plottables will be drawn antialiased, no matter what the specific \hyperlink{a00044_a4fd43e89be4a553ead41652565ff0581}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable\+::set\+Antialiased} value was set to.

if an element in {\itshape not\+Antialiased\+Elements} is already set in \hyperlink{a00116_af6f91e5eab1be85f67c556e98c3745e8}{set\+Antialiased\+Elements}, it is removed from there.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_af6f91e5eab1be85f67c556e98c3745e8}{set\+Antialiased\+Elements} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\hypertarget{a00116_aa0e1c44295da2706d0f12ad48f64b806}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!set\+Range\+Drag@{set\+Range\+Drag}}
\index{set\+Range\+Drag@{set\+Range\+Drag}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{set\+Range\+Drag}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::set\+Range\+Drag (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Qt\+::\+Orientations}]{orientations}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_aa0e1c44295da2706d0f12ad48f64b806}


Sets which axis orientation may be range dragged by the user with mouse interaction. 

What orientation corresponds to which specific axis can be set with \hyperlink{a00116_a9fa10e826a174884391c1c839d52c0a3}{set\+Range\+Drag\+Axes(\+Q\+C\+P\+Axis $\ast$horizontal, Q\+C\+P\+Axis $\ast$vertical)}. By default, the horizontal axis is the bottom axis (x\+Axis) and the vertical axis is the left axis (y\+Axis).

To disable range dragging entirely, pass 0 as {\itshape orientations} or remove i\+Range\+Drag from \hyperlink{a00116_add9cc886ff5257f64fb4117cf6c135fe}{set\+Interactions}. To enable range dragging for both directions, pass {\ttfamily Qt\+::\+Horizontal $\vert$ Qt\+::\+Vertical} as {\itshape orientations}.

In addition to setting {\itshape orientations} to a non-\/zero value, make sure \hyperlink{a00116_add9cc886ff5257f64fb4117cf6c135fe}{set\+Interactions} contains i\+Range\+Drag to enable the range dragging interaction.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_ad4a0919e471549a2daea517ce6538ad8}{set\+Range\+Zoom}, \hyperlink{a00116_a9fa10e826a174884391c1c839d52c0a3}{set\+Range\+Drag\+Axes}, \hyperlink{a00116_a775bdcb6329d44701aeaa6135b0e5265}{set\+No\+Antialiasing\+On\+Drag} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\hypertarget{a00116_ad4a0919e471549a2daea517ce6538ad8}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!set\+Range\+Zoom@{set\+Range\+Zoom}}

\subsubsection[{set\+Range\+Zoom}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::set\+Range\+Zoom (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Qt\+::\+Orientations}]{orientations}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_ad4a0919e471549a2daea517ce6538ad8}


Sets which axis orientation may be zoomed by the user with the mouse wheel. 

What orientation corresponds to which specific axis can be set with \hyperlink{a00116_a9808f1736b8116c116bcccb53cdb210a}{set\+Range\+Zoom\+Axes}(\hyperlink{a00025}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis} $\ast$horizontal, \hyperlink{a00025}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis} $\ast$vertical). By default, the horizontal axis is the bottom axis (x\+Axis) and the vertical axis is the left axis (y\+Axis).

To disable range zooming entirely, pass 0 as {\itshape orientations} or remove i\+Range\+Zoom from \hyperlink{a00116_add9cc886ff5257f64fb4117cf6c135fe}{set\+Interactions}. To enable range zooming for both directions, pass {\ttfamily Qt\+::\+Horizontal $\vert$ Qt\+::\+Vertical} as {\itshape orientations}.

In addition to setting {\itshape orientations} to a non-\/zero value, make sure \hyperlink{a00116_add9cc886ff5257f64fb4117cf6c135fe}{set\+Interactions} contains i\+Range\+Zoom to enable the range zooming interaction.

The two axes can be zoomed with different strengths, when different factors are passed to \hyperlink{a00116_ab0589ec79b1081b13ffb7cf5791a8735}{set\+Range\+Zoom\+Factor(double horizontal\+Factor, double vertical\+Factor)}.

\hypertarget{a00116_ab0589ec79b1081b13ffb7cf5791a8735}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!set\+Range\+Zoom\+Factor@{set\+Range\+Zoom\+Factor}}
\index{set\+Range\+Zoom\+Factor@{set\+Range\+Zoom\+Factor}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{set\+Range\+Zoom\+Factor}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::set\+Range\+Zoom\+Factor (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{double}]{horizontal\+Factor, }
\item[{double}]{vertical\+Factor}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_ab0589ec79b1081b13ffb7cf5791a8735}


Sets how strong one rotation step of the mouse wheel zooms, when range zoom was activated with \hyperlink{a00116_ad4a0919e471549a2daea517ce6538ad8}{set\+Range\+Zoom}. 

The two parameters {\itshape horizontal\+Factor} and {\itshape vertical\+Factor} provide a way to let the horizontal axis zoom at different rates than the vertical axis. Which axis is horizontal and which is vertical, can be set with \hyperlink{a00116_a9808f1736b8116c116bcccb53cdb210a}{set\+Range\+Zoom\+Axes}.

When the zoom factor is greater than one, scrolling the mouse wheel backwards (towards the user) will zoom in (make the currently visible range smaller). For zoom factors smaller than one, the same scrolling direction will zoom out.

\hypertarget{a00116_a4dc31241d7b09680950e19e5f971ed93}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!set\+Selection\+Tolerance@{set\+Selection\+Tolerance}}
\index{set\+Selection\+Tolerance@{set\+Selection\+Tolerance}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{set\+Selection\+Tolerance}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::set\+Selection\+Tolerance (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int}]{pixels}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_a4dc31241d7b09680950e19e5f971ed93}


Sets the tolerance that is used when deciding whether a click on the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} surface selects an object (e.\+g. 

a plottable) or not.

If for example the user clicks in the vicinity of the line of a \hyperlink{a00031}{Q\+C\+P\+Graph}, it's only regarded as a potential selection when the minimum distance between the click position and the graph line is smaller than {\itshape pixels}. Objects that are defined by an area (e.\+g. \hyperlink{a00027}{Q\+C\+P\+Bars}) only react to clicks directly inside the area and ignore this selection tolerance. In other words it only has meaning for parts of objects that are too thin to exactly hit with a click and thus need such a tolerance.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_add9cc886ff5257f64fb4117cf6c135fe}{set\+Interactions}, \hyperlink{a00024_a0fd218d6c4974b6ab05bd2f688818556}{Q\+C\+P\+Abstract\+Plottable\+::select\+Test} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Definition at line \hyperlink{a00115_source_l06352}{6352} of file \hyperlink{a00115_source}{qcustomplot.\+cpp}.

\hypertarget{a00116_a84257c1e1f984b3932245069428f3176}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!set\+Title@{set\+Title}}
\index{set\+Title@{set\+Title}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{set\+Title}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::set\+Title (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Q\+String \&}]{title}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_a84257c1e1f984b3932245069428f3176}


Sets the plot title which will be drawn centered at the top of the widget. 

The title position is not dependant on the actual position of the axes. However, if \hyperlink{a00116_aed5bb30c9b04c1d0103ab8ef7190f23a}{set\+Auto\+Margin} is set to true, the top margin will be adjusted appropriately, so the top axis labels/tick labels will not overlap with the title.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00116_ae104d89b683a6ec6831c4b7b02530f15}{set\+Title\+Font}, \hyperlink{a00116_a57693e1334130e47dae06f8bd226328b}{set\+Title\+Color} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\hypertarget{a00116_ad27d34bcc9e68b5482d128e2f1e38f55}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!setup\+Full\+Axes\+Box@{setup\+Full\+Axes\+Box}}
\index{setup\+Full\+Axes\+Box@{setup\+Full\+Axes\+Box}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{setup\+Full\+Axes\+Box}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::setup\+Full\+Axes\+Box (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_ad27d34bcc9e68b5482d128e2f1e38f55}


Convenience function to make the top and right axes visible and assign them the following properties from their corresponding bottom/left axes\+: 

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item range (\hyperlink{a00025_a57d6ee9e9009fe88cb19db476ec70bca}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis\+::set\+Range}) \item range reversed (\hyperlink{a00025_a2172fdb196b1a0dc3f40992fcad8e9e1}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis\+::set\+Range\+Reversed}) \item scale type (\hyperlink{a00025_adb6c5c45bdf899ea221881dd3b43b406}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis\+::set\+Scale\+Type}) \item scale log base (\hyperlink{a00025_a726186054be90487885a748aa1b42188}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis\+::set\+Scale\+Log\+Base}) \item ticks (\hyperlink{a00025_ac891409315bc379e3b1abdb162c1a011}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis\+::set\+Ticks}) \item auto (major) tick count (\hyperlink{a00025_a7c7111cbeac9ec5fcb40f93a1ef51a0b}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis\+::set\+Auto\+Tick\+Count}) \item sub tick count (\hyperlink{a00025_a4b1554ead9d7f9799650d51383e326dd}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis\+::set\+Sub\+Tick\+Count}) \item auto sub ticks (\hyperlink{a00025_adcbdec7a60054b88571e89599f4a45bf}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis\+::set\+Auto\+Sub\+Ticks}) \item tick step (\hyperlink{a00025_af727db0acc6492c4c774c0700e738205}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis\+::set\+Tick\+Step}) \item auto tick step (\hyperlink{a00025_a99fe77b034e06f5b723995beab96e741}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis\+::set\+Auto\+Tick\+Step})\end{DoxyItemize}
Tick labels (\hyperlink{a00025_a04ba16e1f6f78d70f938519576ed32c8}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis\+::set\+Tick\+Labels}) however, is always set to false.

This function does {\itshape not} connect the range\+Changed signals of the bottom and left axes to the \hyperlink{a00025_a57d6ee9e9009fe88cb19db476ec70bca}{Q\+C\+P\+Axis\+::set\+Range} slots of the top and right axes in order to synchronize the ranges permanently.

\hypertarget{a00116_a953ecdbc28018e7e84cb6213ad3d88c2}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!viewport@{viewport}}
\index{viewport@{viewport}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{viewport}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}Q\+Rect Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::viewport (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}}\label{a00116_a953ecdbc28018e7e84cb6213ad3d88c2}


Returns the viewport rect of this \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} instance. 

The viewport is the area the plot is drawn in, all mechanisms, e.\+g. margin caluclation take the viewport to be the outer border of the plot. The viewport normally is the rect() of the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget, i.\+e. a rect with top left (0, 0) and size of the \hyperlink{a00030_d8/d00/a00186}{Q\+Custom\+Plot} widget.

Don't confuse the viewport with the axis\+Rect. An axis\+Rect is the rect defined by two axes, where the graphs/plottables are drawn in. The viewport is larger and contains also the axes themselves, their tick numbers, their labels, the plot title etc.

Only when saving to a file (see \hyperlink{a00116_a7636261aff1f6d25c9da749ece3fc8b8}{save\+Png}, save\+Pdf etc.) the viewport is temporarily modified to allow saving plots with sizes independent of the current widget size. 

Definition at line \hyperlink{a00116_source_l01957}{1957} of file \hyperlink{a00116_source}{qcustomplot.\+h}.



References \hyperlink{a00116_source_l02110}{m\+Viewport}.


\begin{DoxyCode}
01957 \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \hyperlink{a00116_a69feeea9d5254eab8ba7f9be13f85e0b}{mViewport}; \}
\end{DoxyCode}
\hypertarget{a00116_a7b8bd7e8d3a1d23a8595e9c6a6b76ef1}{\index{qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}!wheel\+Event@{wheel\+Event}}
\index{wheel\+Event@{wheel\+Event}!qcustomplot.\+h@{qcustomplot.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{wheel\+Event}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void Q\+Custom\+Plot\+::wheel\+Event (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Q\+Wheel\+Event $\ast$}]{event}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}}\label{a00116_a7b8bd7e8d3a1d23a8595e9c6a6b76ef1}
Event handler for mouse wheel events. First, the mouse\+Wheel signal is emitted. If range\+Zoom is Qt\+::\+Horizontal, Qt\+::\+Vertical or both, the ranges of the axes defined as range\+Zoom\+Horz\+Axis and range\+Zoom\+Vert\+Axis are scaled. The center of the scaling operation is the current cursor position inside the plot. The scaling factor is dependant on the mouse wheel delta (which direction the wheel was rotated) to provide a natural zooming feel. The Strength of the zoom can be controlled via \hyperlink{a00116_abc0e662d15d41f7262a440818c6885d1}{set\+Range\+Zoom\+Factor}.

Note, that event-\/$>$delta() is usually +/-\/120 for single rotation steps. However, if the mouse wheel is turned rapidly, many steps may bunch up to one event, so the event-\/$>$delta() may then be multiples of 120. This is taken into account here, by calculating {\itshape wheel\+Steps} and using it as exponent of the range zoom factor. This takes care of the wheel direction automatically, by inverting the factor, when the wheel step is negative (f$^\wedge$-\/1 = 1/f). 

Definition at line \hyperlink{a00115_source_l07811}{7811} of file \hyperlink{a00115_source}{qcustomplot.\+cpp}.
